[1/30/2015 8:14:36 ] Пацо: public void paintComponent(Graphics g, int x, int y) {
  super.paintComponent(g);  
  Graphics2D g2 = (Graphics2D) g;
  g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(5f));
  Shape mask = new Ellipse2D.Double(x, y, Game.cellSize + 1, Game.cellSize + 1);
  g2.setPaint(fillMask);
  g2.fill(mask);
  g2.setPaint(borderMask);
  g2.draw(mask);
 };
